"Pending" applicants receive two letters in the mail to explain how to resolve the issue causing their registration to be "pending." #gagop #gapol		Check out this Fact Check--&gt;&gt;	https://t.co/BDuFYENBTo
The "Exact Match" Law is not always the reason for a voting application to be marked "pending." Often, the application is submitted with portions missing or incomplete. When an application is incomplete, the registrant can't be verified.#gagop #gapol		--&gt;&gt;	https://t.co/BDuFYENBTo
When voters fail to provide a form of ID on their application, the identity of the voter cannot be confirmed. Once ID has been provided, the voter can cast a regular ballot. #gagop #gapol		Check out this Fact Check--&gt;&gt;	https://t.co/BDuFYENBTo
"Pending" voter applicants aren't being "held," "purged," or "blocked." Pending voters can complete their applications and show an ID on Election Day and cast a REGULAR ballot. #gagop #gapol		Check out this Fact Check--&gt;&gt;	https://t.co/BDuFYENBTo
